9c:["$","p",null,{"children":["One natural strategy for choosing which correction operation to perform for each syndrome is to choose the ",["$","em",null,{"children":"lowest weight"}]," Pauli operation that, as an error, causes that syndrome.\nThere may in fact be multiple operations that tie for the lowest weight error consistent with a given syndrome, in which case any one of them may be selected.\nThe idea is that lower-weight Pauli operations represent more likely explanations for whatever syndrome has been measured.\nThis might actually not be the case for some noise models, and one alternative strategy is to compute the most ",["$","em",null,{"children":"likely"}]," error that causes the given syndrome, based on the chosen noise model.\nFor this lesson, however, we'll keep things simple and only consider lowest-weight corrections."],"className":"group paragraph-el text-text-primary mx-0"}]
